<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неверующий.html>неве́рующий</a> (25303)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:верующий.html>ве́рующий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vérujuščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неверующий.html>неве́рующий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevérujuščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>unbelieving, disbelieving, nonbelieving</li>
<li>irreligious, faithless</li>
<li>pagan</li>
<li>ungodly</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неверующий.html>неве́рующий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevérujuščij</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неверующий.html>неве́рующего</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неверующий.html>неве́рующие</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неверующий.html>неве́рующих</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неверующий.html>неве́рующая</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>atheist, disbeliever, nonbeliever, unbeliever, pagan, infidel</li></ol>

Гоголь</a>, «<a href = vnd.unilang:письмо.html>Письма</a> 1836—1841 гг.», <span class="example-date">1836—1841</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>г</a>.<span class="citation-source"> <span class="nkrja-source" style="font-size: x-small; font-style: italic;"></span></span></i></span></span></span>} <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen">― Для чего вы, <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">неверующий</span> в истины света и не <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">видящий</span> света, для чего вы пришли сюда, чего хотите вы от нас? <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i><a href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%A2%D0%BE%D0%BB%D1%81%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B9,_%D0%9B%D0%B5%D0%B2_%D0%9D%D0%B8%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%BB%D0%B0%D0%B5%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87" class="extiw" title="w:<a href = vnd.unilang:толстый.html>То́лстой</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:лев.html>Лев</a> Николаевич">Л. Н. Толстой</a>, «Война и мир», <span class="example-date">1867—1869</span> г.<span class="citation-source"> <span class="nkrja-source" style="font-size: x-small; font-style: italic;"></span></span></i></span></span></span> <span style="display: none"><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> |  1 | </a></sup></span><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> |  1 | </a></sup><span style="display: none"><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> |  1 | </a></sup></span><span style="display: none"><sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-4"> | ▼ 1 | </a></sup></span></li>
<li>не признающий существования Бога <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen">И он, он — тоже ослеплённый и <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">неверующий</span>, — он тоже сейчас услышит, он тоже уверует, да, да! <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i><a href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%94%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B5%D0%B2%D1%81%D0%BA%D0%B8%D0%B9,_%D0%A4%D1%91%D0%B4%D0%BE%D1%80_%D0%9C%D0%B8%D1%85%D0%B0%D0%B9%D0%BB%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87" class="extiw" title="w:Достоевский, Фёдор Михайлович">Ф. М. Достоевский</a>, «Преступление и наказание», <span class="example-date">1866</span> г.<span class="citation-source"> <span class="nkrja-source" style="font-size: x-small; font-style: italic;"></span></span></i></span></span></span> <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen">Он, <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">неверующий</span>, стал молиться и в ту минуту, как молился, верил. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i><a href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%A2%D0%BE%D0%BB%D1%81%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B9,_%D0%9B%D0%B5%D0%B2_%D0%9D%D0%B8%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%BB%D0%B0%D0%B5%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87" class="extiw" title="w:<a href = vnd.unilang:толстый.html>То́лстой</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:лев.html>Лев</a> Николаевич">Л. Н. Толстой</a>, «Анна Каренина», <span class="example-date">1878</span> г.<span class="citation-source"> <span class="nkrja-source" style="font-size: x-small; font-style: italic;"></span></span></i></span></span></span> <sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-5"> |  2 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-6"> |  2 | </a></sup><span style="display: none"><sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-7"> |  2 | </a></sup></span><span style="display: none"><sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-8"> | ▼ 2 | </a></sup></span></li>
<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:выступать.html>выступа́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:роль.html>ро́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельного</a>">субстантивир.</span> тот, кто ни во что не верит <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen">В противоположность отцам, дети представляют собой собрание <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">неверующих</span>. — Вы не верите ни во что… даже? — вопрошает Базарова один из Кирсановых. — Даже, — отвечает Базаров, вовсе не заботясь о том, что он делает этот ответ в доме Кирсановых и что, по всем правилам гостеприимства, гость обязан говорить хозяевам лишь приятные и угодные вещи. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i><a href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%A1%D0%B0%D0%BB%D1%82%D1%8B%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%B2-%D0%A9%D0%B5%D0%B4%D1%80%D0%B8%D0%BD,_%D0%9C%D0%B8%D1%85%D0%B0%D0%B8%D0%BB_%D0%95%D0%B2%D0%B3%D1%80%D0%B0%D1%84%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87" class="extiw" title="w:Салтыков-Щедрин, Михаил Евграфович">М. Е. Салтыков-Щедрин</a>, «Сенечкин яд», <span class="example-date">1863—1871</span> г.<span class="citation-source"> <span class="nkrja-source" style="font-size: x-small; font-style: italic;"></span></span></i></span></span></span> <span style="display: none"><sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-9"> |  3 | </a></sup></span><sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-10"> |  3 | </a></sup><span style="display: none"><sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-11"> |  3 | </a></sup></span><span style="display: none"><sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-12"> | ▼ 3 | </a></sup></span></li>
<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:выступать.html>выступа́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:роль.html>ро́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельного</a>">субстантивир.</span> тот, кто не верит в Бога <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen"> — Скажи, о чём ты молишься, Вера? — О <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">неверующих</span>… — тихо сказала она. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i><a href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%93%D0%BE%D0%BD%D1%87%D0%B0%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%B2,_%D0%98%D0%B2%D0%B0%D0%BD_%D0%90%D0%BB%D0%B5%D0%BA%D1%81%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B4%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87" class="extiw" title="w:Гончаров, Иван Александрович">И. А. Гончаров</a>, «Обрыв», <span class="example-date">1869</span> г.<span class="citation-source"> <span class="nkrja-source" style="font-size: x-small; font-style: italic;"></span></span></i></span></span></span> <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen"> — Ты, <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">неверующий</span>, молчи, молчи, пока Бог постучится к тебе в сердце. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i><a href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%9B%D0%B5%D1%81%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%B2,_%D0%9D%D0%B8%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%BB%D0%B0%D0%B9_%D0%A1%D0%B5%D0%BC%D1%91%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87" class="extiw" title="w:<a href = vnd.unilang:лесок.html>Леско́в</a>, Николай Семёнович">Н. С. Лесков</a>, «На ножах», <span class="example-date">1870</span> г.<span class="citation-source"> <span class="nkrja-source" style="font-size: x-small; font-style: italic;"></span></span></i></span></span></span> <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen">И на сердце ни печали, ни досады, ни заботы нет; тут и <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">неверующий</span> в бога поверует. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i><a href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%A1%D0%B0%D0%BB%D1%82%D1%8B%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%B2-%D0%A9%D0%B5%D0%B4%D1%80%D0%B8%D0%BD,_%D0%9C%D0%B8%D1%85%D0%B0%D0%B8%D0%BB_%D0%95%D0%B2%D0%B3%D1%80%D0%B0%D1%84%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87" class="extiw" title="w:Салтыков-Щедрин, Михаил Евграфович">М. <p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">невесёлый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nevesjólyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веселый.html>ве́село</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">véselo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невесело.html>неве́село</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevéselo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>unhappily, sadly</li>

***невеста.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невеста.html>невеста</a> (2704)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nevěsta</i>. Probably from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">not</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведать.html>ве́дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">védatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, indicating a strict hands-off relationship.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невеста.html>неве́ста</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevésta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невеста.html>неве́сты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невеста.html>неве́сты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невеста.html>неве́ст</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fiancée, bride</li>
<li>marriageable girl</li></ol>

***невестка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невестка.html>неве́стка</a> (12076)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невеста.html>неве́ста</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nevésta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">няве́стка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">njavjéstka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невестка.html>неве́стка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevéstka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невестка.html>неве́стки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невестка.html>неве́стки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невестка.html>неве́сток</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a woman’s daughter-in-law <i>(husband’s daughter-in-law is <a href = vnd.unilang:сноха.html>сноха́</a>)</i></li>
<li>sister-in-law <i>(the wife of one’s brother or brother-in-law)</i></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:вест.html>ве́ст</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-невест-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:смекалка.html>-к</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весть.html>весть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, obsolete third singular present indicative of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведать.html>ве́дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">védatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***невзирая.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невзирая.html>невзирая</a> (13824)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взирать.html>взира́я</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzirája</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, present adverbial participle of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взирать.html>взира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzirátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to look, to gaze</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">regardless</i>, literally "without looking".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невзирая.html>невзира́я</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevzirája</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>regardless</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Only used in the expression <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невзирая.html>невзира́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nevzirája na</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">regardless of, despite</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:видать.html>вида́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vidátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щупальце.html>-ль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невидаль.html>не́видаль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">névidalʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невидаль.html>не́видали</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невидаль.html>не́видали</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невидаль.html>не́видалей</a></b>)

***невиданный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невиданный.html>неви́данный</a> (7002)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:виданный.html>ви́данный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vídannyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, past passive participle of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:видать.html>вида́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vidátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невиданный.html>неви́данный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevídannyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неви́даннее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неви́данней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>previously unseen or unknown</li>
<li>extraordinary, exceptional, unprecedented</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ви́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ди.html>ди</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>мый</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невинно.html>невинно</a> (15455)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">неви́нный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nevínnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невинно.html>неви́нно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevínno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>innocently <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">guiltlessly, harmlessly, naively or virginally</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невинно.html>неви́нно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevínno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">неви́нный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nevínnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<ol><li>innocent, not guilty <i>(of)</i>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невнимание.html>невнима́ние</a> (27463)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невнимание.html>невнима́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevnimánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невнимание.html>невнима́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невнимание.html>невнима́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невнимание.html>невнима́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>inattention</li>
<li>disregard, negligence</li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-возвращ-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-ен-ец</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***невозможно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невозможно.html>невозмо́жно</a> (899)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невозможный.html>невозмо́жный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nevozmóžnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невозможно.html>невозмо́жно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevozmóžno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>impossibly</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The predicative <b><a href = vnd.unilang:невозможно.html>невозмо́жно</a></b> is synonymous with <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a></b> with a perfective infinite verb. Thus, sentences with <b><a href = vnd.unilang:невозможно.html>невозмо́жно</a></b> require perfective infinitives.
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>кака́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тяжелый.html>тяжёлая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бочок.html>бо́чка</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Её</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:невозможно.html>невозмо́жно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поднять.html>подня́ть</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kakája tjažólaja bóčka! Jejó <b>nevozmóžno</b> podnjátʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">What a heavy barrel! It's impossible to lift it.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопустимый.html>недопусти́мо</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nedopustímo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nelʹzjá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невозможно.html>невозмо́жно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevozmóžno</span>)
